    			table.insert(t2, k)
    			table.insert(t3, k.CFrame * CFrame.Angles(0, p1 * 1.1, 0))
    		Workspace:BulkMoveTo(t2, t3, Enum.BulkMoveMode.FireCFrameChanged)
    end)

    		t[p1] = {}
    local function remove_tag(p1) --[[ remove_tag | Line: 31 | Upvalues: t (copy) ]]
    	t[p1] = nil
    CollectionService:GetInstanceAddedSignal("slow_rotable_vent"):Connect(add_tag)
    CollectionService:GetInstanceRemovedSignal("slow_rotable_vent"):Connect(remove_tag)

  flashing_light (ModuleScript)
    Path: game.ReplicatedStorage.client.controller.map_details.flashing_light
    --- DECOMPILED CODE ---
    local RuntimeLib = require(game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("include"):WaitForChild("RuntimeLib"))
    local v1 = RuntimeLib.import(script, game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"), "client", "module", "light_util")
    local collect_light_children = v1.collect_light_children
    local get_neon_parent = v1.get_neon_parent
    local play_light_toggle_sound = v1.play_light_toggle_sound
    local set_light_enabled = v1.set_light_enabled
    local TagManager = RuntimeLib.import(script, game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"), "class", "TagManager").TagManager
    local Timer = RuntimeLib.import(script, game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"), "class", "Timer").Timer
    local Timescale = RuntimeLib.import(script, game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"), "module", "namespace", "Timescale").Timescale
    local v2 = Random.new()
    TagManager.new("flickering_light", {
    	add_tag = function(p1, p2) --[[ add_tag | Line: 14 | Upvalues: collect_light_children (copy), get_neon_parent (copy), Timescale (copy), v2 (copy) ]]
    		if p2:IsA("BasePart") then
    			p2.Material = Enum.Material.Neon
    			p1.tagged[p2] = {
    				enabled = true,
    				affected = collect_light_children(p2),
    				neon_parent = get_neon_parent(p2),
    				next_toggle = Timescale.get_time() + v2:NextNumber(0.05, 0.5)
    			}
    	remove_tag = function(p1, p2) --[[ remove_tag | Line: 29 ]]
    		p1.tagged[p2] = nil
    	update = function(p1) --[[ update | Line: 34 | Upvalues: Timescale (copy), set_light_enabled (copy), play_light_toggle_sound (copy), v2 (copy) ]]
    		local v1 = Timescale.get_time()
    		for k, v in pairs(p1.tagged) do
    				if k:GetAttribute("destroyed") == nil then
    					if v.next_toggle <= v1 then
    						v.enabled = not v.enabled
    						set_light_enabled(k, v.affected, v.enabled, v.neon_parent)
    						play_light_toggle_sound(k, v.enabled)
    						v.next_toggle = if v.enabled then v1 + v2:NextNumber(0, 1) ^ 4 * 10 else v1 + v2:NextNumber(0.01, 0.06)
    				set_light_enabled(k, v.affected, false, v.neon_parent)
    }, Timer.new(0.07))
    TagManager.new("brief_flash_light", {
    	add_tag = function(p1, p2) --[[ add_tag | Line: 56 | Upvalues: collect_light_children (copy), get_neon_parent (copy), set_light_enabled (copy), Timescale (copy), v2 (copy) ]]
    		if p2:IsA("BasePart") then
    			local v1 = collect_light_children(p2)
    			local v22 = get_neon_parent(p2)
    			set_light_enabled(p2, v1, false, v22)

    				affected = v1,
    				neon_parent = v22,

    			}

    		p1.tagged[p2] = nil
    	update = function(p1) --[[ update | Line: 80 | Upvalues: Timescale (copy), set_light_enabled (copy), play_light_toggle_sound (copy), v2 (copy) ]]
    		local v1 = Timescale.get_time()

    		if p2:IsA("BasePart") then
    			local v1 = p2:GetAttribute("sound_id")
    				local v3 = p2:GetAttribute("volume") and 1
    				local Sound = Instance.new("Sound")

    				Sound.Parent = SoundService.master.ingame.main.background

    				})

    					entity = v4,
    				}

    		local v1 = p1.tagged[p2]
    			v1.sound:Stop()

    				time_offset = v2:NextNumber(0, v1)
    			}

The AFT MK-16\'s career in USSOCOM was ultimately cut short when it was removed from inventory in 2013 in favor of SOPMOD M4s and 5.56 conversions for the MK-17. Despite this, the MK-16 has not suffered much from this setback, as it has gone on to serve in the special forces and counterterrorism units of various European nations. In game, the Mk. 16 has good ergonomics and generally controllable recoil, but it is also one of the heavier 5.56 rifles even with its more compact setups.",
